        $(function () {
            $.OP.GG.common.GNBAutoComplete.init();

            $('.gnb-btn-dropdown').click(function () {
                var dropdownButton = $(this),
                    dropdownItem = dropdownButton.closest('.gnb-list-item-dropdown');

                dropdownItem.toggleClass('gnb-list-item-dropdown--acitve');

                $(document).on('click', function (event) {
                    var target = event.target || event.srcElement;
                    var $target = $(target);

                    if (!$target.closest('.gnb-list-item-dropdown').length) {
                        dropdownItem.removeClass('gnb-list-item-dropdown--acitve');
                    }
                });
            });

					$tabItem = $tab.find('[class*="item"]');

					_this.addClass(activeClass).siblings().removeClass(activeClass);
				});
			})();

		(function () {

			(function(){
				var $search = $('.c-playersearch'),
					$input = $search.find('.c-playersearch__input-text'),
					$result = $search.find('.c-playerresult'),
					expendClass = 'c-playerresult--is-expend';
				$input.on('focus', function (e) {
					var _this = $(this),
						$thisResult = _this.closest('.c-playersearch').find('.c-playerresult');
					$thisResult.addClass(expendClass);
				});
				$search.on('click', function(e){
					e.stopPropagation();
				});
				$(document).on('click', function(e){
					$result.removeClass(expendClass);
				});


			})();
	});

        $(function(){
		var init = function(){
            $('.opgg-language__list').on('click', function(event){
                setLocale(event);
                var defaultServer = 'KR';

                $(event.target).startLoading({
                    maxHeight: 15
                });

                $.OP.GG.layout.regionLanguage.cookie.seti18n(getCurrentLocale());

                window.location.reload();
            });

            $(".opgg-language__open-short").html(searchLocaleElement(getCurrentLocale()).find('span').html());

            $("html body").on("click", function(e) {
                var $games = $(e.target).closest(".opgg-header__navi-open");
                var $language = $(e.target).closest(".opgg-language__open");
                $(".opgg-header__navi-box")[$games.length ? "toggle" : "hide"]();
                // $(".opgg-language__box")[$language.length ? "toggle" : "hide"]();
            });
        },
        getCurrentLocale = function(){
            return $('.opgg-language__item--is-active').data('locale');
        },
        searchLocaleElement = function(locale){
            if (locale === undefined) {
                locale = getCurrentLocale();
            }

            return $('.opgg-language__list').find('.opgg-language__item[data-locale=' + locale + ']');
        },
        setLocale = function(event){
            var locale = undefined;
            if (event) {
                var $item = $(event.target).closest('.opgg-language__item');
                locale = $item.data('locale');
                $('.opgg-language__item').removeClass('opgg-language__item--is-active');
                $item.addClass('opgg-language__item--is-active');
            }
            $('.opgg-language__open-short')
                .html(
                    searchLocaleElement(locale)
                        .find('span')
                        .html()
                );
        };
        init();
	});

    $(function() {
        var $expandBtn = $('.navi-expand__button');
        var $naviExpand = $('.navi-expand');

        $expandBtn.on('click', function(e) {
            if($naviExpand.hasClass('navi-expand--hide')) {
                $naviExpand.removeClass('navi-expand--hide');
                $naviExpand.addClass('navi-expand--show');
            } else {
                $naviExpand.removeClass('navi-expand--show');
                $naviExpand.addClass('navi-expand--hide');
            }
        });

        $('html body').on('click', function(e) {
             var $navi = $(e.target).closest(".navi-expand__wrapper");
             if(!$navi.length) {
                $naviExpand.removeClass('navi-expand--show');
                $naviExpand.addClass('navi-expand--hide');
             }
        });
    })

    <div class="GameListContainer" data-summoner-id="84531289"
         data-last-info="1617292803">
        <div class="Header Box">
            <style>
	.SelectMatchTypes,
	.ChampionMatchSearchWrap > .Content { display: none; }
</style>
<script>

	$(function(){
		var wrap = $('.ChampionMatchSearchWrap'),
				content = $('>.Content', wrap),
				allChampionList = $(">.SelectMatchChampionList >.Item.All .ChampionList", content);

		var searchInputPast = null;
		var doubleChosungArray = {
			'ㄳ': 'ㄱㅅ',
			'ㄵ': 'ㄴㅈ',
			'ㄶ': 'ㄴㅎ',
			'ㄺ': 'ㄹㄱ',
			'ㄻ': 'ㄹㅁ',
			'ㄼ': 'ㄹㅂ',
			'ㄽ': 'ㄹㅅ',
			'ㄾ': 'ㄹㅌ',
			'ㄿ': 'ㄹㅍ',
			'ㅀ': 'ㄹㅎ',
			'ㅄ': 'ㅂㅅ'
		};

		var updateSearchKeyword = function(oSearchInput){
			var keyword = oSearchInput.val().toLowerCase();
			var allChampionHeader = $(">.AllChampion", allChampionList);
			var allChampions = $(">.Item", allChampionList);

			if (keyword.length > 0) {
				allChampionHeader.show();
			}

//				if (keyword == searchInputPast) {
//					return;
//				}

			for (var doubleChosung in doubleChosungArray) {
				if (doubleChosungArray.hasOwnProperty(doubleChosung)) {
					var spritedChosung = doubleChosungArray[doubleChosung];
					keyword = keyword.replaceAll(doubleChosung, spritedChosung);
				}
			}

			searchInputPast = keyword;

			allChampions.each(function(i, o){
				var championName = $(o).data('champion-name'),
						championKey = $(o).data('champion-key'),
						championNameChosung = $(o).data('champion-name-chosung');

				if (championName) {
					if (championName.indexOf(keyword) >= 0 || championKey.indexOf(keyword) >= 0 || (championNameChosung && championNameChosung.indexOf(keyword) >= 0)) {
						$(o).removeClass('hide');
						$(o).addClass('show');
					} else {
						$(o).removeClass('show');
						$(o).addClass('hide');
					}
				}
			});

			var championNotFound = $(">.ChampionNotFound", allChampionList);
			if ($(">.Item.show", allChampionList).length == 0) {
				championNotFound.show();
			} else {
				championNotFound.hide();
			}
		};

		var showChampionMatchSearch = function(){
					// 중복 이벤트 할당 문제
					if (content.is(':visible')) {
						return;
					}

					content.show();
					$(document).on('click', function(event){
						var target = event.target || event.srcElement;
						if (!$(target).closest(wrap.selector).length) {
							hideChampionMatchSearch();
						}
					});
				},
				hideChampionMatchSearch = function(){
					content.hide();
					$(document).off('click');
				};

		// 아무키나 누르면 띄워주도록
		var searchInput = $('>.Header >.Input', wrap);
		searchInput
				.on('keyup keydown change click', function(){
					 // 엔터키 입력 시 챔피언 리스트 숨길지 컨셉 필요
					showChampionMatchSearch();
					updateSearchKeyword($(this));
					ga('send', 'event', 'button', 'OpenChampionSearchInMatch');
				})
				.keypress(function(event) {
					if (event.charCode === 13) {
						var serachText = $(".ChampionMatchSearchWrap > .Header > .Input")[0].value;
						$(".ChampionList > .Item > .Link").each(function(index, value) {
							if (value.innerHTML.trim().toLowerCase().split(" ").join("") === serachText.trim().toLowerCase().split(" ").join("")) {
								$.OP.GG.matches.list.changeChampion($(value).data('champion-id'));
								 // 엔터키 입력 시 챔피언 리스트 숨길지 컨셉 필요
								$(document).off('click');
								return;
							}
						});
					}
				});
	});
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        var headerButton = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__header--button");
        var headerButtonIcon = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__header--button-icon");
        var content = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__content");
        var footer = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__footer");
        var spinClassName = "opscore-banner__header--button-icon-spin";

        headerButton.onclick = function () {
            headerButtonIcon.classList.toggle(spinClassName);
            content.classList.toggle("hide");
            footer.classList.toggle("hide");
        }
    })();
</script>		<div class="GameItemList">

    <script>
        $(function () {
            var $gameItemList = $('.GameListContainer');

            $gameItemList.on('click', '.AlertMessageButton .Button', function (evt) {
                evt.preventDefault();
                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                var summonerId = $gameItem.data('summoner-id');
                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');

                if ($this.hasClass('Blue')) {
                    $.OP.GG.summoner.renewBtn.start(evt.currentTarget, summonerId);
                } else if ($this.hasClass('Green')) {
                    $.OP.GG.summoner.RequireRenewMatch(summonerId, gameId, evt.currentTarget);
                }
            });

            $gameItemList.on('click', '.OpenBuildButton', function (evt) {
                evt.preventDefault();
                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                var summonerId = $gameItem.data('summoner-id');
                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');

                $.OP.GG.matches.openBuild(gameId, summonerId, $gameItem);
            });

            $gameItemList.on('click', '.OpenSpectateButton', function (evt) {
                evt.preventDefault();
                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');

                $.OP.GG.matches.openSpectate(gameId);
            });

            $gameItemList.on('click', '.Button.MatchDetail', function (evt) {
                evt.preventDefault();
                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                var summonerId = $gameItem.data('summoner-id');
                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');
                var gameTime = $gameItem.data('game-time');
                var gameResult = $gameItem.data('game-result');

                if ($gameItem.hasClass('extended') === false)
                    $.OP.GG.tracker.combine.sendEvent(['FB', 'Pixel'], 'Summoner-Detail', 'Show', {gameResult: gameResult});

                $.OP.GG.matches.openDetail(gameId, summonerId, $gameItem, gameTime);
            })
        });
    </script>

	<script>
		window.lifeOnwer = function(){
			this.randAdIdx = '61109482';
			this.showAd = function(element, size){
				if (size === "skyscraper") {
					this.showAdSkyscraper();
					return;
				}
				element.innerHTML = this.getAdHTML(size);
				element.classList.remove('vm-placement');
			};

			this.showAdSkyscraper = function(){
				if (this.getMobileOS() !== "unknown") {
					return;
				}

				var elementLeft = document.createElement("div");
				elementLeft.innerHTML = this.getAdHTML("skyscraper");
				elementLeft.setAttribute('style', 'position: absolute; left: 50%; top: 372px; margin-left: -725px;');
				document.body.appendChild(elementLeft);

				var elementRight = document.createElement("div");
				elementRight.innerHTML = this.getAdHTML("skyscraper");
				elementRight.setAttribute('style', 'position: absolute; right: 50%; top: 372px; margin-right: -725px;');
				document.body.appendChild(elementRight);

				$(elementRight).scrollToFixed({
					marginTop: 60
				});
			};

			this.getAdHTML = function(size){
				var lang = (this.getLang() === 'ko_KR' ? 'ko' : 'en');
				return "<a href=\"" + this.getAdLink(this.adIndex) + "\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"lifeOnwer-" + randAdIdx + "\">" +
					"<img src='//opgg-static.akamaized.net/images/lifeowner/opgg/" + lang + "/" + adIndex + "-" + size + ".png'>" +
					"</a>";
			};
			this.getAdLink = function(adIndex){
				var linkKey = this.getMobileOS() + '-' + adIndex;
				switch (linkKey) {
					case "Android-1":
						return "market://details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner01%26utm_content%3Dapp";
					case "Android-2":
						return "market://details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner02%26utm_content%3Dlol";
					case "Android-3":
						return "market://details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3banner03%26utm_content%3Dpubg";
					case "unknown-1":
						return "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner01%26utm_content%3Dapp";
					case "unknown-2":
						return "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner02%26utm_content%3Dlol";
					case "unknown-3":
						return "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner03%26utm_content%3Dpubg";
					default:
						return "itms-apps://itunes.apple.com/kr/app/apple-store/id605722237";
				}
			};
			this.getMobileOS = function(){
				var userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor;

				if (/android/i.test(userAgent)) {
					return "Android";
				}

				if (/iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(userAgent)) {
					return "iOS";
				}

				return "unknown";
			};
			this.getLang = function(){
				return document.documentElement.lang || "en";
			};

			this.slots = [
				{
					'id': '5a84644f46e0fb0001d74d3c',
					'size': '970x90'
				},
				{
					'id': '5a84640c46e0fb0001fc3bb0',
					'size': '300x250'
				},
				{
					'id': '5a8462a746e0fb0001bf35aa',
					'size': 'skyscraper'
				},
			];
			this.getCookie = function(name){
				var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
				if (match) return match[2];
			};
			this.bindClickEvent = function(){
				$(".lifeOnwer-" + randAdIdx).click(function(evt){
					$.OP.GG.tracker.combine.sendEvent(['FB', 'Pixel'], 'Opgg', 'ClickAd', {
						Location: location_,
						subLocation: subLocation,
						BannerType: adIndex
					});
				});
			};

			this.adIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * (this.getMobileOS() === "iOS" ? 2 : 3)) + 1;
			this.location_ = "summoner";
			this.subLocation = "summary";


			slots.forEach(function(slot){
				if (self.getMobileOS() === "unknown" && slot.size === "300x250") {
					return;
				}
				var element = document.querySelector('.vm-placement[data-id="' + slot.id + '"]');
				if (element) {
					self.showAd(element, slot.size);
				}
			});
			this.bindClickEvent();
		};
	</script>
